e

 These documents reveal conspiracies to carry out Mumbai-like attacks in Europe
 yah film ek memory discs main maujuud thi
 CNN quoted intelligence sources as saying that these documents contained terrorist training programs in PDF format in German, English, and Arabic languages
 sienen ne kaha he ki german samachar patr 'daai jeit' ne sabase pehle in dastavejon ke paae jane ke bare main rapat prakashit kii thi
 These documents were found by German cryptographic experts inside a memory disk found near a suspected Al Qaeda terrorist arrested in Berlin last year
 22 varshiya austrian makasuud lodin se poochtacha kar rahe jaanchakarta uske janghie ke neeche chupa ek digital bhandaaran upkaran or memory cards paakar dang rah gaye
 Lodin had recently returned to Pakistan via Budapest, Hungary, and then reached Germany
 in upkarnon ken andar ek ashleel video dafan tha, jiskaa sheershak 'kik es' tha or ek file thi, jiskaa sheershak 'sexi tanja' tha
 Several weeks later, German investigators discovered a treasure trove of secret information contained within the original video, which contained over 100 documents from Al Qaeda
 sienen ne kaha he ki 'future works' sheershak vaala ek dastavej lagata he ki hamale ke nae lakshyon va tareekon kii talash par hui charchaaon se sambandhit he
 German investigators believe the document was prepared in 2009
 dastavej taiyaar kiye jane ke ek varsh baad europea khufia agenciyaan mumbai hamale jaise ek hamale kii sajeesh kii jaanch ke liye haath-paanv maar rahi thim, jisamen german va anya europea aatankwaadiyon ke shaamil hone kii ashanka thi

 "I think it is reasonable to think that the 'future Works' document is part of that particular project," quoted Yasin Musharbash, investigative journalist for Die Zeit, who released the first report on these documents

 " CNN has stated that 'fuser Works' does not have any date or place, or plan, but it seems to be a suggestive discussion of taking new initiatives, and bringing Al Qaeda back into the spotlight around the world

 UGC

 Scholarship Process- The student has taken admission in any full-time professional course for post graduation

 Police find a boy and girl bled near the Naranpur railway gate in Ahmedabad
 ladkaa bataata he ki sharaab ke nashe main dhutt chaar ladakon ne raat ke andhere main uski garlfriend ke saath gangrape kii koshish kii or jab unhone virodh kiya to badmaashon ne donon ko jakhmi kar diya
 But right now the police are investigating that suddenly a suicide note causes the whole matter to stand on its head
 ahmedabad ke police control room ke paas ek phone aata he
 The caller says that a boy and a girl are found dead near the Naranpura crossing on the saurashtra-ahmedabad railway track
 khabar milte hi police fouran maukey par ravaanaa ho jaati he
 In a short time, the police of Naranpura police station is on the scene
 yahaan telephone par di gai jaankaree ke mutabik ek ladkaa or ladki railway trek ke najadik lahooluhaan haalat main pade hue mil jate hai, lekin buree tarah jakhmi hone ke baavjood donon jinda the
 The police immediately pick up both of them and take them to the hospital without losing any time, but at the Civil Hospital in Ahmedabad, the girl dies while undergoing treatment at night, while the condition of the boy is still critical
 isi dauraan police ko ye pataa chalata he ki donon hi railway trek ke bagal main pade hone ke baavjood kisi train kii chapet main aane se jakhmi nahin hue, balki unhen kisi ne chaakuon se god kar lahooluhaan kar diya tha
 The attackers attacked the girl in the stomach with knives about five to six times and the boy was stabbed once
 haalanki is cese main police ko tab pehali baar thodi hairaani hui, jab usne is vaardaat ke bare main telephone par jaankaree denevaale shaks se dobaaraa baat karne kii koshish kii, kyonki tab kar kol karanevaale shaks kaa mobile phone rahasyamayi tareeke se band ho chukaa tha
 Now, to understand the whole incident, the police starts questioning the young man who was victim of the incident and with this he narrates a shocking story
 mul rup se maharashtra ke raigarh kaa rahanevaala 26 saal kaa noujvaan birbal prasad bataata he ki wo apni premika ke saath vaardaat ke vakt naranpura railway crossing ke nazadik ghoomane ke liye gaya tha, lekin achaanak jhaadiyon se sharaab ke nashe main dhutt chaar noujvaan unke saamne aa gaye or unhone uski premika ke saath badsuluki shuru kar di
 Tried to gang-rape her, on opposing them, the four attacked them with knives, but when this attack worsened their girlfriend's condition, all four left them on the spot and fled
 
 puri ghatana rongte khadey karanevaali thi
 a story that would have been on anyone's hearing would be reminiscent of the December 16 gang rape in Delhi, but here the police were constantly knocking many things
 unamem se ek to lakh koshish ke baavjood is ghatana kii khabar denevaale shaks se police kii baat nahin ho paane kii thi or doosraa ek ghaney rihaayshi ilaake ke bich se guzaranevaale is railway trek ke bich itani badi vaardaat kaa hone ke baavjood iske bare main kaanon-kaan kisi ko khabar tak nahin mili
 The police could not interrogate the boy who was injured due to the injury, but when the police examined his clothes and belongings, a paper part from his bag suddenly cleared the whole story
 Because this part was nothing but a suicide note
 lekin agar ye dabl suicide kii koshish thi, to wo ladke koun the, jinhone in donon ke saath zyaadati karne kii koshish kii? to kya gangrape kii koshish or chaakubazi kii wo kahani banaavati thi? aakhir kyon?ghayal ladke ke bag se mila suicide note puri kahani ko palat chukaa tha
 Meanwhile, the police came to know another shocking thing
 usne dekha ki ladke ke pet main chaaku kaa ek gaharaa waar to maujuud he, lekin naa to uske jacket par chaaku laga he, naa hi shart par or naa baniyaan par
 Now the question was, how can an attacker finally stab someone in his stomach without spoiling his clothes? When the police got a suicide note from one of these two boys, the whole story was almost cleared
 ladke ke bag se mili is suicide note main likhaa tha ki wo jo kaam karne ja rahaa he, wo sharmnaak or ghinauna he, lekin chunki use ladke ke gharavaalon ne bahut jaleel kiya he
 Therefore, he is compelled to do so
 is suicide note se ab ye baat takreeban saaf lag rahi thi ki shaayad ladke ne hi apni premika par chaakuon se hamalaa karne ke baad khud ko bhi chaaku maar kar jaan lene kii koshish kii or jab is koshish main wo naakaam ho gaya, to usne khud ko kaanoon kii nazaron se bachaane ke liye bilkul dilli ke 16 disambar ke jaisi ek kahani bana lee
 The police had already suspected the boy, but the getting of the suicide note, the stabbing of the knives, many of the bags in the story
 ye tamaam chizein police ke shaq ko yakeen main tabdeel kar rahi thi par tabhi saamne aae ek or subut ne police ko puri tarah santusht kar diya
 This was proof, the mobile phone which was switched off after calling the police
 police ne jab chaanbin kii, to ye mobile phone khudakushi kii koshish karanevaale birbal prasad kaa hi niklaa or uske paas se hi baraamad ho gaya
 That is, after hitting his girlfriend and himself with knives, Birbal himself called the police and told about himself and tried to confuse him
 takneekee jagat main har roj kuch nayaa ho rahaa he
 Our progress and your life are also being greatly affected by this progress
 kuch myanon main ye prabhaav sakaaratmak he or kuch myanon main nakaaratmak
 Along with us, the life of our children has not remained untouched by this
 mahaj do saal kii umr main ve mobile, tablet va computer main is kadar kho jate hai ki khud ko aasapaas ke maahaul se alag kar lete hai
 This affects their mental and physical development
 chaar saal kii arunima ne ek saal pehle pehali baar mobile phone apane haath main liya tha
 After this, in her colorful display, she lost so much that after school and during holidays, her only companion is the same mobile

 This episode presents the story of Vasudev Balwant Phadke
 vasudev balavant fadake kii daastaan- vasudev balavant fadake kaa janm 4 november, 1845 ko maharashtra ke raigarh jile ke shirdhone gaanv main hua tha
 Phadke was the first revolutionary of India to organize an armed rebellion against the British government
 - unhone 1857 ke pratham swatantraaa sangram kii vifaltaa ke baad azaadi ke mahasamar kii pehali chinagaari jalaai thi
 After his early education, his father wanted him to work in a shop, but he did not listen to his father and came to Mumbai
 - unhone jangal main ek abhyaas sthal banaaya, jahaan jyotiba phule or lokmaanya tilak bhi unke saathi the
 Here people were made to practice arms
 - 1871 main unako soochna mili kii unki maa kii tabiyat kharaab he, un dinon wo angrejon kii ek company main kaam kar rahe the
 He went to seek leave but could not be found
 - avkaash nahin milane ke baad bhi fadake apane gaanv chale gaye, lekin tab tak maa kii mrityu ho chuki thi
 This incident filled his mind with anger against the British
 - fadake ne naukari chhod di
 Started preparing for revolution against the British
 unhen adivaasiyon kii sena sangathit karne kii koshish shuru kar di
 In 1879, he declared a revolt against the British
 paise ekatra karne ke liye kai jagahon par daake bhi daalane shuru kiye
 - Vasudev Phadke's influence had spread in seven districts of Maharashtra
 unki gatividhi se angrej afasar dar gaye the

 - angrej sarkaar ne vasudev fadake ko jinda yaa murda pakadaney par 50 hajaar rupee kaa inaam ghoshit kiya
 The British followed them
 - 20 july, 1879 ko fadake beemaari kii haalat main ek mandir main aaraam kar rahe the
 At the same time, he was arrested
 - unke khilaaf rajdroh kaa mukadmaa chalaaya gaya or kalapani kii sajaa dekar andaman bhej diya gaya

 Let's know something special related to the life of this great artist: 1
 1925 ko indore main janme walker kaa asli naam badaruddin jamaluddin kaaji tha
 He was a bus conductor before joining the film industry
 2unke pita srinagar main ek kapadaa mil main majdoor the
 When the textile mill closed, the whole family moved to Mumbai
 pita ke liye apane 15 sadasyeey parivaar kaa bharan-poshan karnaa mushkil ho rahaa tha
 To reduce the burden on his father's shoulders, Badruddin continued to try his hand in various occupations, including working as a conductor in the Bombay Electric Supply and Transport (BEST) buses
 3
 At the age of 27, he was primarily posted at Dadar Bus Depot
 badaruddin bas main yatriyon kaa tikat kaatane ke alaava ajeebogareeb kisse-kahaniyaan sunaakar yatriyon kaa man bahalaate rahete

 unki yah ichha puri bhi hui
 Actor Balraj Sahni, who wrote the screenplay for Gurudutt's film 'baaji', caught sight of Badruddin during a bus journey
 4
 Sahni suggested Badruddin to try his luck with Guru Dutt
